# PR #318: Major Borg Fixes & Loadout Improvements

- **Author:** AMcilraith
- **Link:** https://github.com/epic-new-soj-thing/Sojourn-Iskhod/pull/318

## About The Pull Request
<details>
<summary>About The Pull Request</summary>
<hr>

Refactored **Borg Armor** to be more durable and mechanically consistent with other armor in the game.
- Implemented a proper armor resistance system for cyborgs (Melee, Bullet, Laser, etc.) instead of just flat brute/burn reduction.
- Rebalanced existing armor tiers:
    - **Mark I**: Increased HP to 150.
    - **Mark II**: 200 HP. Anti-Laser/Energy focus.
    - **Mark III**: 200 HP. Anti-Melee/Physical focus.
    - **Mark IV**: Renamed to **Heavy Armor Plating** (300 HP, Low Resistances).
    - **Mark V**: Renamed to **Specialized Armor Plating** (250 HP, Good Resistances).
- Added **Mark VI Experimental Armor Plating**: A high-end armor (350 HP, High Resistances) craftable only by the **Artificers Guild**.
- Added **Universal Grippers**: Replaced all specialized grippers (Mining, Engineering, etc.) with a pair of Universal Grippers that can hold almost any item.
- Fixed an issue where **Mop Buckets** were difficult to interact with.

Made several quality-of-life improvements to loadout options and storage accessibility.
- **Church Sheath** is now available to all players in the loadout menu (previously restricted).
- **Pill Bottles** and **IFAKs** can now be accessed from inside containers at any nesting depth (removed storage depth restrictions).
- **Wall-mounted Fire Extinguisher Cabinets** now always spawn with a basic fire extinguisher (previously had randomized spawns including a chance to be empty).
<hr>
</details>

## Changelog
```
:cl:
add: Added 'Universal Gripper' to all Cyborg modules, replacing specialized grippers.
add: Added 'Mark VI Experimental Armor Plating', craftable by the Artificers Guild.
add: Added 'church sheath' as a loadout option available to all players.
balance: Refactored Borg Armor mechanics to use proper damage resistance types (Melee, Bullet, Laser, etc.).
balance: Increased HP of all Borg Armor tiers to be more durable.
balance: Renamed 'Mark IV' to 'Heavy Armor Plating' and 'Mark V' to 'Specialized Armor Plating'.
tweak: Pill bottles and IFAKs can now be accessed and opened from inside containers without depth restrictions.
fix: Fixed Mop Buckets ignoring interactions from mops.
fix: Wall-mounted fire extinguisher cabinets now always spawn with a fire extinguisher instead of sometimes being empty.
/:cl:
```

**Changelog entries (included in build):**

- **add:** Added 'Universal Gripper' to all Cyborg modules, replacing specialized grippers.
- **add:** Added 'Mark VI Experimental Armor Plating', craftable by the Artificers Guild.
- **add:** Added 'church sheath' as a loadout option available to all players.
- **balance:** Refactored Borg Armor mechanics to use proper damage resistance types (Melee, Bullet, Laser, etc.).
- **balance:** Increased HP of all Borg Armor tiers to be more durable.
- **balance:** Renamed 'Mark IV' to 'Heavy Armor Plating' and 'Mark V' to 'Specialized Armor Plating'.
- **tweak:** Pill bottles and IFAKs can now be accessed and opened from inside containers without depth restrictions.
- **fix:** Fixed Mop Buckets ignoring interactions from mops.
- **fix:** Wall-mounted fire extinguisher cabinets now always spawn with a fire extinguisher instead of sometimes being empty.

+/obj/item/gripper/universal/grip_item(obj/item/I as obj, mob/user as mob, var/feedback = 1)
+	if(istype(I, /obj/item/gripper))
+		if(feedback)
+			to_chat(user, "<span class='warning'>You cannot put a gripper inside another gripper. That would be silly.</span>")
+		return FALSE
+
+	if(I.w_class > ITEM_SIZE_BULKY)
+		if(feedback)
+			to_chat(user, "<span class='warning'>The [I] is too large for your universal gripper.</span>")
+		return FALSE
+
+	//It's universal, so we just check if it's already holding something
+	if (!wrapped)
+		if (feedback)
+			to_chat(user, "You collect \the [I].")
+		I.do_pickup_animation(user.loc, I.loc)
+		I.forceMove(src)
+		wrapped = I
+		update_icon()
+		return TRUE
+
+	if (feedback)
+		to_chat(user, "<span class='danger'>Your gripper is already holding \the [wrapped].</span>")
+	return FALSE
+

 /mob/living/silicon/robot/bullet_act(var/obj/item/projectile/Proj)
+	var/datum/robot_component/armor/A = get_armor()
+	if(A && A.armor && A.armor["bullet"] && istype(Proj, /obj/item/projectile/bullet))
+		//Standard armor deflection logic
+		var/chance = A.armor["bullet"]
+		var/obj/item/projectile/bullet/B = Proj
+		if(B.armor_divisor)
+			chance = max((chance / B.armor_divisor), 0)
+
+		if(prob(chance))
+			if (!(Proj.testing))
+				visible_message(SPAN_DANGER("\The [Proj.name] ricochets off [src]\'s armor!"))
+				var/multiplier = round(10 / get_dist(B.starting, src))
+				var/turf/sourceloc = get_turf_away_from_target_complex(src, B.starting, multiplier)
+				if(sourceloc)
+					var/distance = get_dist(sourceloc, src)
+					var/new_x =  sourceloc.x + ( rand(0, distance) * prob(50) ? -1 : 1 )
+					var/new_y =  sourceloc.y + ( rand(0, distance) * prob(50) ? -1 : 1 )
+					B.redirect(new_x, new_y, get_turf(src), src)
+				return PROJECTILE_CONTINUE
+
 	if(HasTrait(CYBORG_TRAIT_DEFLECTIVE_BALLISTIC_ARMOR) && istype(Proj, /obj/item/projectile/bullet))
 		var/chance = 90
